<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пума.html>пу́ма</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">púma</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пума.html>пу́мы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пума.html>пу́мы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пума.html>пу́м</a></b>)

<p>Through <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">punkt</i> and/or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Punkt</i> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">punctum</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***пунцовый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пунцовый.html>пунцо́вый</a> (16156)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Through <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">рąsоwу</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">ponceau</i>, a derivation of <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">paon</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">peacock</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pāvō</i>. Compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:павлин.html>павли́н</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pavlín</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">паун</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">paun</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пунцовый.html>пунцо́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">puncóvyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>crimson</li></ol>

***пуп.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пуп.html>пуп</a> (18128)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">пупъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pupŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pǫpъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bud, navel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пуп.html>пуп</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pup</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пуп.html>пупа́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пуп.html>пупы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пуп.html>пупо́в</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">пупко́вый</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пупочный.html>пупо́чный</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">пупови́чный</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пупок.html>пупо́к</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> belly button, navel, umbilicus
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глупый.html>глуп</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пуп.html>пуп</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">glup kak <b>pup</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">silly (humorous)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пуп.html>пуп</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:земля.html>земли́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pup zemlí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">centre of the world (figuratively)</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">navel of the world</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пурга.html>пурга́</a> (7725)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Likely from a Finno-Ugric language. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Karelian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Karelian language">Karelian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="krl">purgu</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Khanty_language" class="extiw" title="w:Khanty language">Khanty</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="kca">пуркэ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="kca-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">purkè</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mansi_language" class="extiw" title="w:Mansi language">Mansi</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="mns">па̄рк</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="mns-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pārk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пурга.html>пурга́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">purgá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пурга.html>пурги́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пурга.html>пурги́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пурга.html>пург</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>blizzard, snowstorm</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пурпурный.html>пурпурный</a> (23660)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пу́рпур</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">púrpur</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Tyrian purple, crimson</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">purple</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пурпурный.html>пу́рпурный</a></strong> <i>or</i> <strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пурпурный.html>пурпу́рный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">púrpurnyj</span> <i>or</i> <span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">purpúrnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Tyrian purple <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">relating to the dye</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пурпурный.html>пу́рпурная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мастерская.html>мастерска́я</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>púrpurnaja</b> masterskája</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Tyrian purple</b> dyer's workshop</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>crimson, purple</li>
<li>magenta <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. in the CMYK color model</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chemistry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> purpuric</li></ol>

***пуск.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пуск.html>пуск</a> (14048)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пуск.html>пуск</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pusk</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пуск.html>пу́ска</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пуск.html>пуска́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пуск.html>пуско́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>startup <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">act</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>launch</li></ol>

***пускать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пускать.html>пуска́ть</a> (1465)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пускать.html>пуска́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">puskátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустить.html>пусти́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to let go, to relinquish</li>
<li>to set going, to set in motion, to set in operation, to start, to set working</li>
<li>to let in</li>
<li>to launch, to throw</li>
<li>to sprout, to put out, to put forth</li></ol>

***пускаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пускаться.html>пуска́ться</a> (13219)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пускать.html>пуска́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">puskátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пускаться.html>пуска́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">puskátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пуститься.html>пусти́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to start, to set out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пускаться.html>пуска́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>путь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>puskátʹsja</b> v putʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to start on a journey</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пускаться.html>пуска́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вдогонку.html>вдого́нку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> ке́м-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>puskátʹsja</b> vdogónku za kém-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to rush/dash after someone (in pursuit of someone)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пускаться.html>пуска́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тяжкий.html>тя́жкие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">puskátʹsja vo vse tjážkije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">1) to plunge into dissipation; 2) to go to all lengths, stop short at nothing</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to start
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пускаться.html>пуска́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бежать.html>бежа́ть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>puskátʹsja</b> bežátʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to break into a run; start running</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пускаться.html>пуска́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рискованный.html>риско́ванное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:предприятие.html>предприя́тие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>puskátʹsja</b> v riskóvannoje predprijátije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to let oneself in for a risky undertaking</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to go <i>(into)</i>, to plunge <i>(into)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пускаться.html>пуска́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подробность.html>подро́бности</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>puskátʹsja</b> v podróbnosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go into detail(s)/particulars</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пускаться.html>пуска́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пространный.html>простра́нные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:объяснение.html>объясне́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>puskátʹsja</b> v prostránnyje obʺjasnénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to start lengthy explanations</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пускаться.html>пуска́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спора.html>спо́ры</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>puskátʹsja</b> v spóry</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to plunge into argument</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:пускаться.html>пуска́ться</a></strong></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">puskátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пусковой.html>пусково́й</a> (23379)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пуск.html>пуск</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pusk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ово́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пусковой.html>пусково́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">puskovój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> starting, launching, launch
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пусковой.html>пусково́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:двигатель.html>дви́гатель</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>puskovój</b> dvígatelʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>starter</b> motor</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пусковой.html>пускова́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:петля.html>пе́тля</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>puskovája</b> pétlja</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/launch_loop" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:launch loop"><b>launch</b> loop</a></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пусковой.html>пускова́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:установка.html>устано́вка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>puskovája</b> ustanóvka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">launcher</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>launching</b> device</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пустеть.html>пусте́ть</a> (16927)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустой.html>пусто́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pustój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-еть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-etʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустеть.html>пусте́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pustétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опустеть.html>опусте́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to become empty</li>
<li>to become deserted</li></ol>

***пустить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пустить.html>пусти́ть</a> (1420)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pustìti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустить.html>пусти́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pustítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пускать.html>пуска́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to let <i>(go)</i>, to allow, to permit, to release</li>
<li>to set going, to set in motion, to set in operation, to start, to set working</li>
<li>to let in</li>
<li>to launch, to throw</li>
<li><i>(botany)</i> to sprout, to put out, to put forth</li></ol>

***пуститься.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пуститься.html>пусти́ться</a> (7188)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустить.html>пусти́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pustítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пуститься.html>пусти́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pustítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пускаться.html>пуска́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to start, to set out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пуститься.html>пусти́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>путь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pustítʹsja</b> v putʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to start on a journey</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пуститься.html>пусти́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вдогонку.html>вдого́нку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> ке́м-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pustítʹsja</b> vdogónku za kém-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to rush/dash after someone (in pursuit of someone)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пуститься.html>пусти́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тяжкий.html>тя́жкие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pustítʹsja vo vse tjážkije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">1) to plunge into dissipation; 2) to go to all lengths, stop short at nothing</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to start
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пуститься.html>пусти́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бежать.html>бежа́ть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pustítʹsja</b> bežátʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to break into a run; start running</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пуститься.html>пусти́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рискованный.html>риско́ванное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:предприятие.html>предприя́тие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pustítʹsja</b> v riskóvannoje predprijátije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to let oneself in for a risky undertaking</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to go <i>(into)</i>, to plunge <i>(into)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пуститься.html>пусти́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подробность.html>подро́бности</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pustítʹsja</b> v podróbnosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go into detail(s)/particulars</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пуститься.html>пусти́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пространный.html>простра́нные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:объяснение.html>объясне́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pustítʹsja</b> v prostránnyje obʺjasnénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to start lengthy explanations</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пуститься.html>пусти́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спора.html>спо́ры</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pustítʹsja</b> v spóry</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to plunge into argument</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустить.html>пусти́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pustítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***пустой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пустой.html>пустой</a> (567)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">поустъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pustŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pustъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустой.html>пусто́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pustój</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)пусте́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:пустеть.html>пусте́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>empty, void, hollow
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переливать.html>перелива́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пустой.html>пусто́го</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:порожний.html>поро́жнее</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">perelivatʹ iz pustóvo v poróžneje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to beat the air to mill the wind</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пустой.html>пусты́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>рука́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s pustými rukámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">empty-handed</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустой.html>пуста́я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:порода.html>поро́да</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pustája poróda</i> ― <span class="e-translation">barren rock</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>idle <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of talk</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>shallow <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of one's personality</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>futile, frivolous</li>
<li>vain, ungrounded</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порожний.html>поро́жний</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poróžnij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pustyni</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустой.html>пусто́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pustój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ы́ня</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ýnja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустыня.html>пусты́ня</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pustýnja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустыня.html>пусты́ни</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустыня.html>пусты́ни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустыня.html>пусты́нь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>desert, wilderness</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> unpopulated area</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пустырь.html>пусты́рь</a> (6398)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустырь.html>пусты́рь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pustýrʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустырь.html>пустыря́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустырь.html>пустыри́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустырь.html>пустыре́й</a></b>)
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустышка.html>пусты́шка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pustýška</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустышка.html>пусты́шки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустышка.html>пусты́шки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустышка.html>пусты́шек</a></b>)

***пусть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пусть.html>пусть</a> (299)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пускать.html>пуска́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">puskátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Particle">Particle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пусть.html>пусть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pustʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>let + subject + conjugated verb
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пусть.html>Пусть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>пи́шет</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Pustʹ</b> on píšet</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Let</b> him write.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пусть.html>Пусть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:думать.html>ду́мает</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>ней</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:забыть.html>забы́ли</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Pustʹ</b> oná ne dúmajet, što my o nej zabýli.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Let</b> her not think that we forgot about her.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пусть.html>пусть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pustʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>though, even (if), although
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хороший.html>хоро́ший</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работник.html>рабо́тник</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пусть.html>пусть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:своенравный.html>своенра́вный</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On xoróšij rabótnik, <b>pustʹ</b> i svojenrávnyj</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He’s a good worker, <b>although</b> crotchety.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> let
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пусть.html>пусть</a></b> X (<a href = vnd.unilang:икс.html>икс</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:равно.html>равно́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>двум</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pustʹ</b> X (iks) ravnó dvum</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>let</b> X be 2</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:путавший.html>пу́тавший</a> (5778)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:путаница.html>пу́таница</a> (9695)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:путаница.html>пу́таница</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pútanica</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:путаница.html>пу́таницы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:путаница.html>пу́таницы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:путаница.html>пу́таниц</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>confusion, hash <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">confused mess</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>muddiness</li>
<li>mess, muss</li>
<li>tangle, maze, snarl</li>
<li>mix</li>
<li>jumble</li>
<li>mishmash</li>
<li>mingle-mangle</li>
<li>imbroglio</li>
<li>embroilment</li>
<li>disorder</li>
<li>mull</li>
<li>bewilderment</li></ol>
